connection_matrices/incast/gen_random_incast_8192n_2c_0us_1Ms.cm
!Experiment incast 200 Gbps  1 MB 2 connections 0 startdelta algorithm rccc
!Binary ./htsim_uec
!Param -linkspeed 200000
!Param -topo topologies/leaf_spine_8192_200g.topo
!Param -q 50
!Param -ecn  12   37
!Param -cwnd 75
!tailFCT 112
!Param -end 224
